I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[BUG] DynamoDB Enhanced Client initial null Boolean field does not get updated on update_item
## Service

DynamoDB

## AWS API Action

put_item() followed by an update_item() using Spring Boot 4.0.5 and AWS SDK version 2.42.30 and Kotlin 2.3.20

## Expected behavior

When putting an item with put_item in DDB with an optional Boolean field, and then setting the boolean field to true and using update_item to have the row being updated with boolean value true.
 

## Actual behavior

When retrieving the item after above scenario, the boolean field value is still null.

## Reproduction

Python example that mimics what enhanced client does:
```
import boto3
from botocore.config import Config

# Configure boto3 to use Floci
endpoint_url = "http://localhost:4566"
region = "us-east-1"

dynamodb = boto3.client(
    'dynamodb',
    endpoint_url=endpoint_url,
    region_name=region,
    aws_access_key_id='test',
    aws_secret_access_key='test',
    config=Config(signature_version='v4')
)

TABLE_NAME = "test-boolean-fix"


def setup_table():
    """Create the test table."""
    try:
        dynamodb.delete_table(TableName=TABLE_NAME)
        print(f"Deleted existing table: {TABLE_NAME}")
    except dynamodb.exceptions.ResourceNotFoundException:
        pass

    dynamodb.create_table(
        TableName=TABLE_NAME,
        KeySchema=[
            {'AttributeName': 'userId', 'KeyType': 'HASH'}
        ],
        AttributeDefinitions=[
            {'AttributeName': 'userId', 'AttributeType': 'S'}
        ],
        ProvisionedThroughput={
            'ReadCapacityUnits': 5,
            'WriteCapacityUnits': 5
        }
    )
    print(f"Created table: {TABLE_NAME}")


def test_boolean_update_with_set_and_remove():
    """
    Test that demonstrates the fix for boolean updates with SET and REMOVE combined.
    Which the Java SDK v2 enhanced client does underwater. There's no boto3 equivalent of that enhanced client.

    This mimics what the DynamoDB Enhanced Client does when ignoreNulls=false:
    - SET non-null fields
    - REMOVE null fields

    The bug was: the last SET attribute before REMOVE was not being set correctly
    because the parser included part of the REMOVE clause in the value lookup.
    """
    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("Test: Boolean update with SET and REMOVE combined")
    print("="*60)

    user_id = "user-123"

    # Step 1: Create item WITHOUT the boolean field
    print("\n1. Creating item WITHOUT isActive field...")
    dynamodb.put_item(
        TableName=TABLE_NAME,
        Item={
            'userId': {'S': user_id},
            'entries': {'S': 'initial entries'},
            'created': {'N': '1234567890'},
            'tempField': {'S': 'to be removed'}
        }
    )

    # Verify initial state
    response = dynamodb.get_item(
        TableName=TABLE_NAME,
        Key={'userId': {'S': user_id}}
    )
    item = response.get('Item', {})
    print(f"   Initial item: {item}")
    assert 'isActive' not in item, "isActive should not exist initially"
    assert 'tempField' in item, "tempField should exist initially"
    print("   ✓ Initial state verified")

    # Step 2: Update with SET and REMOVE combined (like Enhanced Client does)
    print("\n2. Updating with SET and REMOVE combined...")
    print("   UpdateExpression: SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created")

    update_response = dynamodb.update_item(
        TableName=TABLE_NAME,
        Key={'userId': {'S': user_id}},
        UpdateExpression="SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created",
        ExpressionAttributeNames={
            '#entries': 'entries',
            '#isActive': 'isActive',
            '#tempField': 'tempField',
            '#created': 'created'
        },
        ExpressionAttributeValues={
            ':entries': {'S': 'updated entries'},
            ':isActive': {'BOOL': True}
        },
        ReturnValues='ALL_NEW'
    )

    updated_item = update_response.get('Attributes', {})
    print(f"   Updated item: {updated_item}")

    # Verify the update response
    assert 'isActive' in updated_item, "isActive should exist after update"
    assert updated_item['isActive'].get('BOOL') == True, "isActive should be True"
    assert updated_item['entries']['S'] == 'updated entries', "entries should be updated"
    assert 'tempField' not in updated_item, "tempField should be removed"
    assert 'created' not in updated_item, "created should be removed"
    print("   ✓ Update response verified")

    # Step 3: Get the item to verify persistence
    print("\n3. Getting item to verify persistence...")
    response = dynamodb.get_item(
        TableName=TABLE_NAME,
        Key={'userId': {'S': user_id}}
    )
    final_item = response.get('Item', {})
    print(f"   Final item: {final_item}")

    assert final_item['isActive'].get('BOOL') == True, "isActive should still be True after get"
    print("   ✓ Persistence verified")

    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("✓ TEST PASSED: Boolean update with SET and REMOVE works correctly!")
    print("="*60)


def test_boolean_update_from_false_to_true():
    """
    Test updating a boolean from false to true with SET and REMOVE.
    """
    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("Test: Boolean update from false to true")
    print("="*60)

    user_id = "user-456"

    # Step 1: Create item WITH isActive = false
    print("\n1. Creating item with isActive = false...")
    dynamodb.put_item(
        TableName=TABLE_NAME,
        Item={
            'userId': {'S': user_id},
            'entries': {'S': 'initial'},
            'isActive': {'BOOL': False},
            'tempField': {'S': 'temp'}
        }
    )

    response = dynamodb.get_item(
        TableName=TABLE_NAME,
        Key={'userId': {'S': user_id}}
    )
    item = response.get('Item', {})
    assert item['isActive'].get('BOOL') == False, "isActive should be False initially"
    print("   ✓ Initial state: isActive = False")

    # Step 2: Update isActive to true with REMOVE clause
    print("\n2. Updating isActive to true with REMOVE clause...")
    update_response = dynamodb.update_item(
        TableName=TABLE_NAME,
        Key={'userId': {'S': user_id}},
        UpdateExpression="SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField",
        ExpressionAttributeNames={
            '#entries': 'entries',
            '#isActive': 'isActive',
            '#tempField': 'tempField'
        },
        ExpressionAttributeValues={
            ':entries': {'S': 'updated'},
            ':isActive': {'BOOL': True}
        },
        ReturnValues='ALL_NEW'
    )

    updated_item = update_response.get('Attributes', {})
    assert updated_item['isActive'].get('BOOL') == True, "isActive should be True after update"
    print("   ✓ Update response: isActive = True")

    # Step 3: Verify persistence
    print("\n3. Verifying persistence...")
    response = dynamodb.get_item(
        TableName=TABLE_NAME,
        Key={'userId': {'S': user_id}}
    )
    final_item = response.get('Item', {})
    assert final_item['isActive'].get('BOOL') == True, "isActive should still be True"
    print("   ✓ Persistence verified: isActive = True")

    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("✓ TEST PASSED: Boolean update from false to true works!")
    print("="*60)


def cleanup():
    """Delete the test table."""
    try:
        dynamodb.delete_table(TableName=TABLE_NAME)
        print(f"\nCleaned up table: {TABLE_NAME}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Cleanup warning: {e}")


if __name__ == '__main__':
    try:
        setup_table()
        test_boolean_update_with_set_and_remove()
        test_boolean_update_from_false_to_true()
        print("\n" + "="*60)
        print("ALL TESTS PASSED!")
        print("="*60)
    except AssertionError as e:
        print(f"\n✗ TEST FAILED: {e}")
        exit(1)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n✗ ERROR: {e}")
        exit(1)
    finally:
        cleanup()

```
Result with v1.5.1 of Floci:
✗ TEST FAILED: isActive should exist after update


Pseudo-code Kotlin:
```
@DynamoDbBean
class SomeData {
  var uid: String? = null
  var textField: String? = null
  var booleanField: Boolean? = null
}

@SpringBootTest
@AutoConfigureMockMvc
class IntegrationTest {

  @Test
  fun `Test container behaviour`() {
    val uid = UUID.randomUUID().toString()
    val someData = SomeData()
    someData.uid = uid
    ddb.putItem(someData)

   // As expected, only uid is not null
    assertThat(db.getItem(uid)!!.booleanField).isNull()
    assertThat(db.getItem(uid)!!.uid).isNotNull()
    assertThat(db.getItem(uid)!!.textField).isNull()

   someData.textField = "abc"
   someData.booleanField = true
   ddb.updateItem(someData)

    // Expecting all fields to not be null and the boolean field to be true but that test fails
    assertThat(db.getItem(uid)!!.uid).isNotNull()
    assertEquals("abc", db.getItem(uid)!!.textField)
    assertEquals(true, db.getItem(uid)!!.booleanField)  <-- fails

}
```

- mavenBom "software.amazon.awssdk:bom:2.42.30".  Also happens with v2.42.24.
- Kotlin 2.3.20

    24	import java.util.List;
    25	import java.util.Map;
    26	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
    27	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentSkipListMap;
    28	
    29	@ApplicationScoped
    30	public class DynamoDbService {
    31	
    32	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(DynamoDbService.class);
    33	
    34	    private final StorageBackend<String, TableDefinition> tableStore;
    35	    private final StorageBackend<String, Map<String, JsonNode>> itemStore;
    36	    // Items stored per table: storageKey -> Map<itemKey, item>
    37	    // itemKey is "pk" or "pk#sk" depending on table schema
    38	    private final ConcurrentHashMap<String, ConcurrentSkipListMap<String, JsonNode>> itemsByTable = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    39	    private final RegionResolver regionResolver;
    40	    private DynamoDbStreamService streamService;
    41	
    42	    @Inject
    43	    public DynamoDbService(StorageFactory storageFactory, RegionResolver regionResolver,
    44	                           DynamoDbStreamService streamService) {
    45	        this(storageFactory.create("dynamodb", "dynamodb-tables.json",
    46	                new TypeReference<Map<String, TableDefinition>>() {}),
    47	             storageFactory.create("dynamodb", "dynamodb-items.json",
    48	                new TypeReference<Map<String, Map<String, JsonNode>>>() {}),
    49	             regionResolver, streamService);
    50	    }

    52	    /** Package-private constructor for testing. */
    53	    DynamoDbService(StorageBackend<String, TableDefinition> tableStore) {
    54	        this(tableStore, null, new RegionResolver("us-east-1", "000000000000"), null);
    55	    }

    58	        this(tableStore, null, regionResolver, null);
    59	    }

    61	    DynamoDbService(StorageBackend<String, TableDefinition> tableStore,
    62	                    StorageBackend<String, Map<String, JsonNode>> itemStore,
    63	                    RegionResolver regionResolver) {
    64	        this(tableStore, itemStore, regionResolver, null);

    66	
    67	    DynamoDbService(StorageBackend<String, TableDefinition> tableStore,
    68	                    StorageBackend<String, Map<String, JsonNode>> itemStore,
    69	                    RegionResolver regionResolver,
    70	                    DynamoDbStreamService streamService) {
    71	        this.tableStore = tableStore;
    72	        this.itemStore = itemStore;
    73	        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
    74	        this.streamService = streamService;
    75	        loadPersistedItems();
    76	    }
    77	
    78	    private void loadPersistedItems() {
    79	        if (itemStore == null) return;
    80	        for (String key : itemStore.keys()) {
    81	            itemStore.get(key).ifPresent(items ->
    82	                itemsByTable.put(key, new ConcurrentSkipListMap<>(items)));
    83	        }
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    private void persistItems(String storageKey) {
    87	        if (itemStore == null) return;
    88	        var items = itemsByTable.get(storageKey);
    89	        if (items != null) {
    90	            itemStore.put(storageKey, new HashMap<>(items));
    91	        } else {
    92	            itemStore.delete(storageKey);
    93	        }
    94	    }

    96	    public TableDefinition createTable(String tableName,
    97	                                        List<KeySchemaElement> keySchema,
    98	                                        List<AttributeDefinition> attributeDefinitions,
    99	                                        Long readCapacity, Long writeCapacity) {
   100	        return createTable(tableName, keySchema, attributeDefinitions, readCapacity, writeCapacity,
   101	                           List.of(), List.of(), regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   102	    }

   105	                                        List<KeySchemaElement> keySchema,
   106	                                        List<AttributeDefinition> attributeDefinitions,
   107	                                        Long readCapacity, Long writeCapacity, String region) {
   108	        return createTable(tableName, keySchema, attributeDefinitions, readCapacity, writeCapacity,
   109	                           List.of(), List.of(), region);
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    public TableDefinition createTable(String tableName,
   113	                                        List<KeySchemaElement> keySchema,
   114	                                        List<AttributeDefinition> attributeDefinitions,
   115	                                        Long readCapacity, Long writeCapacity,
   116	                                        List<GlobalSecondaryIndex> gsis, String region) {
   117	        return createTable(tableName, keySchema, attributeDefinitions, readCapacity, writeCapacity,
   118	                           gsis, List.of(), region);
   119	    }
   120	
   121	    public TableDefinition createTable(String tableName,
   122	                                        List<KeySchemaElement> keySchema,
   123	                                        List<AttributeDefinition> attributeDefinitions,
   124	                                        Long readCapacity, Long writeCapacity,
   125	                                        List<GlobalSecondaryIndex> gsis,
   126	                                        List<LocalSecondaryIndex> lsis,
   127	                                        String region) {
   128	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   129	        if (tableStore.get(storageKey).isPresent()) {
   130	            throw new AwsException("ResourceInUseException",
   131	                    "Table already exists: " + tableName, 400);
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        TableDefinition table = new TableDefinition(tableName, keySchema, attributeDefinitions,
   135	                region, regionResolver.getAccountId());
   136	        if (readCapacity != null && writeCapacity != null) {
   137	            table.getProvisionedThroughput().setReadCapacityUnits(readCapacity);
   138	            table.getProvisionedThroughput().setWriteCapacityUnits(writeCapacity);
   139	        }
   140	
   141	        if (gsis != null && !gsis.isEmpty()) {
   142	            for (GlobalSecondaryIndex gsi : gsis) {
   143	                gsi.setIndexArn(table.getTableArn() + "/index/" + gsi.getIndexName());
   144	            }
   145	            table.setGlobalSecondaryIndexes(new ArrayList<>(gsis));
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        if (lsis != null && !lsis.isEmpty()) {
   149	            String tablePk = table.getPartitionKeyName();
   150	            for (LocalSecondaryIndex lsi : lsis) {
   151	                String lsiPk = lsi.getPartitionKeyName();
   152	                if (!tablePk.equals(lsiPk)) {
   153	                    throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   154	                            "LocalSecondaryIndex partition key must match table partition key", 400);
   155	                }
   156	                lsi.setIndexArn(table.getTableArn() + "/index/" + lsi.getIndexName());
   157	            }
   158	            table.setLocalSecondaryIndexes(new ArrayList<>(lsis));
   159	        }
   160	
   161	        tableStore.put(storageKey, table);
   162	        itemsByTable.put(storageKey, new ConcurrentSkipListMap<>());
   163	        LOG.infov("Created table: {0} in region {1}", tableName, region);
   164	        return table;
   165	    }
   166	
   167	    public TableDefinition describeTable(String tableName) {
   168	        return describeTable(tableName, regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   169	    }
   170	
   171	    public TableDefinition describeTable(String tableName, String region) {
   172	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   173	        TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey)
   174	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));
   175	
   176	        // Update dynamic counts
   177	        var items = itemsByTable.get(storageKey);
   178	        if (items != null) {
   179	            table.setItemCount(items.size());
   180	        }
   181	        return table;
   182	    }
   183	
   184	    public void deleteTable(String tableName) {
   185	        deleteTable(tableName, regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   186	    }
   187	
   188	    public void deleteTable(String tableName, String region) {
   189	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   190	        if (tableStore.get(storageKey).isEmpty()) {
   191	            throw resourceNotFoundException(tableName);
   192	        }
   193	        tableStore.delete(storageKey);
   194	        itemsByTable.remove(storageKey);
   195	        if (itemStore != null) {
   196	            itemStore.delete(storageKey);
   197	        }
   198	        if (streamService != null) {
   199	            streamService.deleteStream(tableName, region);
   200	        }
   201	        LOG.infov("Deleted table: {0}", tableName);
   202	    }
   203	
   204	    public List<String> listTables() {
   205	        return listTables(regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   206	    }
   207	
   208	    public List<String> listTables(String region) {
   209	        String prefix = region + "::";
   210	        return tableStore.scan(k -> k.startsWith(prefix)).stream()
   211	                .map(TableDefinition::getTableName)
   212	                .toList();
   213	    }

   216	        putItem(tableName, item, null, null, null, regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   217	    }
   218	
   219	    public void putItem(String tableName, JsonNode item, String region) {
   220	        putItem(tableName, item, null, null, null, region);
   221	    }
   222	
   223	    public void putItem(String tableName, JsonNode item,
   224	                         String conditionExpression,
   225	                         JsonNode exprAttrNames, JsonNode exprAttrValues,
   226	                         String region) {
   227	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   228	        TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey)
   229	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));
   230	
   231	        String itemKey = buildItemKey(table, item);
   232	        var tableItems = itemsByTable.computeIfAbsent(storageKey, k -> new ConcurrentSkipListMap<>());
   233	
   234	        JsonNode existing = tableItems.get(itemKey);
   235	
   236	        if (conditionExpression != null) {
   237	            evaluateCondition(existing, conditionExpression, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues);
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        tableItems.put(itemKey, item);
   241	        persistItems(storageKey);
   242	        LOG.debugv("Put item in {0}: key={1}", tableName, itemKey);
   243	
   244	        if (streamService != null) {
   245	            streamService.captureEvent(tableName,
   246	                    existing == null ? "INSERT" : "MODIFY", existing, item, table, region);
   247	        }
   248	    }
   249	
   250	    public JsonNode getItem(String tableName, JsonNode key) {
   251	        return getItem(tableName, key, regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   252	    }
   253	
   254	    public JsonNode getItem(String tableName, JsonNode key, String region) {
   255	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   256	        TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey)
   257	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));
   258	
   259	        String itemKey = buildItemKey(table, key);
   260	        var items = itemsByTable.get(storageKey);
   261	        if (items == null) return null;
   262	        JsonNode item = items.get(itemKey);
   263	        if (item != null && isExpired(item, table)) return null;
   264	        return item;
   265	    }

   267	    public JsonNode deleteItem(String tableName, JsonNode key) {
   268	        return deleteItem(tableName, key, null, null, null, regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   269	    }

   271	    public JsonNode deleteItem(String tableName, JsonNode key, String region) {
   272	        return deleteItem(tableName, key, null, null, null, region);
   273	    }
   274	
   275	    public JsonNode deleteItem(String tableName, JsonNode key,
   276	                                String conditionExpression,
   277	                                JsonNode exprAttrNames, JsonNode exprAttrValues,
   278	                                String region) {
   279	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   280	        TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey)
   281	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));
   282	
   283	        String itemKey = buildItemKey(table, key);
   284	        var items = itemsByTable.get(storageKey);
   285	        if (items == null) return null;
   286	
   287	        if (conditionExpression != null) {
   288	            JsonNode existing = items.get(itemKey);
   289	            evaluateCondition(existing, conditionExpression, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues);
   290	        }
   291	
   292	        JsonNode removed = items.remove(itemKey);
   293	        persistItems(storageKey);
   294	        LOG.debugv("Deleted item from {0}: key={1}", tableName, itemKey);
   295	
   296	        if (streamService != null && removed != null) {
   297	            streamService.captureEvent(tableName, "REMOVE", removed, null, table, region);
   298	        }
   299	
   300	        return removed;
   301	    }

   319	    public UpdateResult updateItem(String tableName, JsonNode key, JsonNode attributeUpdates,
   320	                                    String updateExpression,
   321	                                    JsonNode expressionAttrNames, JsonNode expressionAttrValues,
   322	                                    String returnValues, String conditionExpression, String region) {
   323	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   324	        TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey)
   325	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));
   326	
   327	        String itemKey = buildItemKey(table, key);
   328	        var items = itemsByTable.computeIfAbsent(storageKey, k -> new ConcurrentSkipListMap<>());
   329	
   330	        // Get existing item or create new one from key
   331	        JsonNode existing = items.get(itemKey);
   332	
   333	        if (conditionExpression != null) {
   334	            evaluateCondition(existing, conditionExpression, expressionAttrNames, expressionAttrValues);
   335	        }

   337	        ObjectNode item;

   352	                var entry = fields.next();

   877	    private void applyUpdateExpression(ObjectNode item, String expression,
   878	                                        JsonNode exprAttrNames, JsonNode exprAttrValues) {
   879	        // Parse SET and REMOVE clauses from expressions like:
   880	        // "SET #n = :newName, age = :newAge REMOVE oldField"
   881	        String remaining = expression.trim();
   882	
   883	        while (!remaining.isEmpty()) {
   884	            String upper = remaining.toUpperCase();
   885	            if (upper.startsWith("SET ")) {
   886	                remaining = remaining.substring(4).trim();
   887	                remaining = applySetClause(item, remaining, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues);
   888	            } else if (upper.startsWith("REMOVE ")) {
   889	                remaining = remaining.substring(7).trim();
   890	                remaining = applyRemoveClause(item, remaining, exprAttrNames);
   891	            } else if (upper.startsWith("ADD ")) {
   892	                remaining = remaining.substring(4).trim();
   893	                remaining = applyAddClause(item, remaining, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues);
   894	            } else if (upper.startsWith("DELETE ")) {
   895	                // DELETE is for sets — skip for now
   896	                break;
   897	            } else {
   898	                break;
   899	            }
   900	        }
   901	    }
   902	
   903	    private String applySetClause(ObjectNode item, String clause,
   904	                                   JsonNode exprAttrNames, JsonNode exprAttrValues) {
   905	        // Parse comma-separated assignments: "attr = :val, #name = :val2"
   906	        // Stop when we hit another clause keyword (REMOVE, ADD, DELETE) or end
   907	        while (!clause.isEmpty()) {
   908	            String upper = clause.toUpperCase();
   909	            if (upper.startsWith("REMOVE ") || upper.startsWith("ADD ") || upper.startsWith("DELETE ")) {
   910	                break;
   911	            }
   912	
   913	            // Parse "attrPath = valueExpr"
   914	            int eqIdx = clause.indexOf('=');
   915	            if (eqIdx < 0) break;
   916	
   917	            String attrPath = clause.substring(0, eqIdx).trim();
   918	            String attrName = resolveAttributeName(attrPath, exprAttrNames);
   919	
   920	            String rest = clause.substring(eqIdx + 1).trim();
   921	
   922	            // Find the value placeholder or expression
   923	            String valuePart;
   924	            int commaIdx = findNextComma(rest);
   925	            if (commaIdx >= 0) {
   926	                valuePart = rest.substring(0, commaIdx).trim();
   927	                rest = rest.substring(commaIdx + 1).trim();
   928	            } else {
   929	                // Check for next clause keyword
   930	                int nextClause = findNextClauseKeyword(rest);
   931	                if (nextClause >= 0) {
   932	                    valuePart = rest.substring(0, nextClause).trim();
   933	                    rest = rest.substring(nextClause).trim();
   934	                } else {
   935	                    valuePart = rest.trim();
   936	                    rest = "";
   937	                }
   938	            }
   939	
   940	            // Resolve the value
   941	            if (valuePart.startsWith("if_not_exists(")) {
   942	                // if_not_exists(attrRef, fallbackExpr) evaluates to:
   943	                //   attrRef's current value  — when attrRef exists in the item
   944	                //   fallbackExpr             — otherwise
   945	                // The result is always assigned to attrName.
   946	                String[] args = extractFunctionArgs(valuePart);
   947	                if (args.length == 2) {
   948	                    String checkAttr = resolveAttributeName(args[0].trim(), exprAttrNames);
   949	                    String fallbackExpr = args[1].trim();
   950	                    JsonNode resolved;
   951	                    if (item.has(checkAttr)) {
   952	                        // attrRef exists — evaluate to its current value
   953	                        resolved = item.get(checkAttr);
   954	                    } else if (fallbackExpr.startsWith(":") && exprAttrValues != null) {
   955	                        resolved = exprAttrValues.get(fallbackExpr);
   956	                    } else {
   957	                        // fallback is itself an attribute reference
   958	                        resolved = item.get(resolveAttributeName(fallbackExpr, exprAttrNames));
   959	                    }
   960	                    if (resolved != null) {
   961	                        item.set(attrName, resolved);
   962	                    }
   963	                }
   964	            } else if (valuePart.startsWith("list_append(")) {
   965	                String[] args = extractFunctionArgs(valuePart);
   966	                if (args.length == 2) {
   967	                    String arg1 = args[0].trim();
   968	                    String arg2 = args[1].trim();

  1152	    private int findNextComma(String s) {
  1153	        // Find next comma that is not inside a function call
  1154	        int depth = 0;
  1155	        for (int i = 0; i < s.length(); i++) {
  1156	            char c = s.charAt(i);
  1157	            if (c == '(') depth++;
  1158	            else if (c == ')') depth--;
  1159	            else if (c == ',' && depth == 0) return i;
  1160	        }
  1161	        return -1;
  1162	    }
  1163	
  1164	    private int findNextClauseKeyword(String s) {
  1165	        // Find the start of the next clause keyword (SET, REMOVE, ADD, DELETE)
  1166	        String upper = s.toUpperCase();
  1167	        int[] positions = {
  1168	            indexOfKeyword(upper, "SET "),
  1169	            indexOfKeyword(upper, "REMOVE "),
  1170	            indexOfKeyword(upper, "ADD "),
  1171	            indexOfKeyword(upper, "DELETE ")
  1172	        };
  1173	        int min = -1;
  1174	        for (int pos : positions) {
  1175	            if (pos >= 0 && (min < 0 || pos < min)) {
  1176	                min = pos;
  1177	            }
  1178	        }
  1179	        return min;
  1180	    }
  1181	
  1182	    private int indexOfKeyword(String upper, String keyword) {
  1183	        int idx = upper.indexOf(keyword);
  1184	        // Ensure it's at word boundary (start of string or preceded by space)
  1185	        if (idx > 0 && upper.charAt(idx - 1) != ' ') return -1;
  1186	        return idx;
  1187	    }

   291	    @Test
   292	    void queryWithFilterExpressionAndLimitUsesPreFilterPageState() {
   293	        createOrdersTable();
   294	
   295	        ObjectNode first = item("customerId", "c1", "orderId", "o1");
   296	        first.set("total", attributeValue("N", "100"));
   297	        service.putItem("Orders", first);
   298	
   299	        ObjectNode second = item("customerId", "c1", "orderId", "o2");
   300	        second.set("total", attributeValue("N", "99"));
   301	        service.putItem("Orders", second);
   302	
   303	        ObjectNode third = item("customerId", "c1", "orderId", "o3");
   304	        third.set("total", attributeValue("N", "100"));
   305	        service.putItem("Orders", third);
   306	
   307	        ObjectNode exprValues = mapper.createObjectNode();
   308	        exprValues.set(":pk", attributeValue("S", "c1"));
   309	        exprValues.set(":min", attributeValue("N", "100"));
   310	
   311	        DynamoDbService.QueryResult firstPage = service.query("Orders", null, exprValues,
   312	                "customerId = :pk", "total >= :min", 2, null, null, null, null, "us-east-1");
   313	
   314	        assertEquals(1, firstPage.items().size());
   315	        assertEquals("o1", firstPage.items().get(0).get("orderId").get("S").asText());
   316	        assertEquals(2, firstPage.scannedCount());
   317	        assertNotNull(firstPage.lastEvaluatedKey());
   318	        assertEquals("o2", firstPage.lastEvaluatedKey().get("orderId").get("S").asText());
   319	
   320	        DynamoDbService.QueryResult secondPage = service.query("Orders", null, exprValues,
   321	                "customerId = :pk", "total >= :min", 2, null, null,
   322	                firstPage.lastEvaluatedKey(), null, "us-east-1");
   323	
   324	        assertEquals(1, secondPage.items().size());
   325	        assertEquals("o3", secondPage.items().get(0).get("orderId").get("S").asText());
   326	        assertEquals(1, secondPage.scannedCount());
   327	        assertNull(secondPage.lastEvaluatedKey());
   328	    }

   505	    void updateItemSetIfNotExistsCopiesSourceAttributeWhenAttrNameDiffersFromCheckAttr() {
   506	        // SET a = if_not_exists(b, :v) where b exists → a must be set to b's current value
   507	        createUsersTable();
   508	
   509	        // Put an item that has "source" but not "target"
   510	        ObjectNode existing = mapper.createObjectNode();

   515	        service.putItem("Users", existing);
   516	
   517	        ObjectNode key = item("userId", "u-copy");
   518	
   519	        ObjectNode exprValues = mapper.createObjectNode();
   520	        ObjectNode fallbackVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); fallbackVal.put("S", "fallback");
   521	        exprValues.set(":v", fallbackVal);
   522	
   523	        // target = if_not_exists(source, :v) — source exists, so target should receive source's value

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.InMemoryStorage;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.DynamoDbService;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.AttributeDefinition;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.KeySchemaElement;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.TableDefinition;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.util.List;

public class ReproduceTest {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        DynamoDbService service = new DynamoDbService(new InMemoryStorage<>());
        ObjectMapper mapper = new ObjectMapper();
        
        // Create table
        service.createTable("test-boolean-fix",
                List.of(new KeySchemaElement("userId", "HASH")),
                List.of(new AttributeDefinition("userId", "S")),
                5L, 5L);
        
        // Step 1: Create item WITHOUT the boolean field (like the PR description)
        ObjectNode putItem = mapper.createObjectNode();
        ObjectNode userIdVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); userIdVal.put("S", "user-123");
        ObjectNode entriesVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); entriesVal.put("S", "initial entries");
        ObjectNode createdVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); createdVal.put("N", "1234567890");
        ObjectNode tempFieldVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); tempFieldVal.put("S", "to be removed");
        putItem.set("userId", userIdVal);
        putItem.set("entries", entriesVal);
        putItem.set("created", createdVal);
        putItem.set("tempField", tempFieldVal);
        service.putItem("test-boolean-fix", putItem);
        
        // Verify initial state
        ObjectNode key = mapper.createObjectNode();
        ObjectNode keyUserId = mapper.createObjectNode(); keyUserId.put("S", "user-123");
        key.set("userId", keyUserId);
        JsonNode initial = service.getItem("test-boolean-fix", key);
        System.out.println("Initial item: " + initial);
        System.out.println("isActive present initially: " + (initial != null && initial.has("isActive")));
        System.out.println("tempField present initially: " + (initial != null && initial.has("tempField")));
        
        // Step 2: Update with SET and REMOVE combined (like Enhanced Client does)
        // "SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created"
        ObjectNode exprAttrNames = mapper.createObjectNode();
        exprAttrNames.put("#entries", "entries");
        exprAttrNames.put("#isActive", "isActive");
        exprAttrNames.put("#tempField", "tempField");
        exprAttrNames.put("#created", "created");
        
        ObjectNode exprAttrValues = mapper.createObjectNode();
        ObjectNode newEntries = mapper.createObjectNode(); newEntries.put("S", "updated entries");
        ObjectNode isActiveTrue = mapper.createObjectNode(); isActiveTrue.put("BOOL", true);
        exprAttrValues.set(":entries", newEntries);
        exprAttrValues.set(":isActive", isActiveTrue);
        
        String updateExpression = "SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created";
        
        System.out.println("\nApplying update expression: " + updateExpression);
        
        DynamoDbService.UpdateResult updateResult = service.updateItem(
            "test-boolean-fix", key, null,
            updateExpression, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues, "ALL_NEW");
        
        System.out.println("Update result attributes: " + updateResult.attributes());
        
        // Step 3: Get the item to verify persistence
        JsonNode finalItem = service.getItem("test-boolean-fix", key);
        System.out.println("\nFinal item: " + finalItem);
        System.out.println("isActive present in final: " + (finalItem != null && finalItem.has("isActive")));
        if (finalItem != null && finalItem.has("isActive")) {
            System.out.println("isActive value: " + finalItem.get("isActive"));
            System.out.println("isActive BOOL: " + finalItem.get("isActive").get("BOOL"));
        }
        System.out.println("entries value: " + (finalItem != null ? finalItem.get("entries") : "null"));
        System.out.println("tempField present: " + (finalItem != null && finalItem.has("tempField")));
        System.out.println("created present: " + (finalItem != null && finalItem.has("created")));
        
        // Check if the bug is present
        if (finalItem == null || !finalItem.has("isActive") || !finalItem.get("isActive").has("BOOL") || finalItem.get("isActive").get("BOOL").asBoolean() != true) {
            System.out.println("\nBUG REPRODUCED: isActive should be true but is not!");
            System.exit(1);
        } else {
            System.out.println("\nTEST PASSED: isActive correctly set to true!");
        }
    }
}

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/ReproduceTest.java << 'EOF'
package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb;

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.InMemoryStorage;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.AttributeDefinition;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.KeySchemaElement;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.util.List;

public class ReproduceTest {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        DynamoDbService service = new DynamoDbService(new InMemoryStorage<>());
        ObjectMapper mapper = new ObjectMapper();
        
        // Create table
        service.createTable("test-boolean-fix",
                List.of(new KeySchemaElement("userId", "HASH")),
                List.of(new AttributeDefinition("userId", "S")),
                5L, 5L);
        
        // Step 1: Create item WITHOUT the boolean field
        ObjectNode putItem = mapper.createObjectNode();
        ObjectNode userIdVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); userIdVal.put("S", "user-123");
        ObjectNode entriesVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); entriesVal.put("S", "initial entries");
        ObjectNode createdVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); createdVal.put("N", "1234567890");
        ObjectNode tempFieldVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); tempFieldVal.put("S", "to be removed");
        putItem.set("userId", userIdVal);
        putItem.set("entries", entriesVal);
        putItem.set("created", createdVal);
        putItem.set("tempField", tempFieldVal);
        service.putItem("test-boolean-fix", putItem);
        
        // Verify initial state
        ObjectNode key = mapper.createObjectNode();
        ObjectNode keyUserId = mapper.createObjectNode(); keyUserId.put("S", "user-123");
        key.set("userId", keyUserId);
        JsonNode initial = service.getItem("test-boolean-fix", key);
        System.out.println("Initial item: " + initial);
        System.out.println("isActive present initially: " + (initial != null && initial.has("isActive")));
        System.out.println("tempField present initially: " + (initial != null && initial.has("tempField")));
        System.out.println("created present initially: " + (initial != null && initial.has("created")));
        
        // Step 2: Update with SET and REMOVE combined (like Enhanced Client does)
        // "SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created"
        ObjectNode exprAttrNames = mapper.createObjectNode();
        exprAttrNames.put("#entries", "entries");
        exprAttrNames.put("#isActive", "isActive");
        exprAttrNames.put("#tempField", "tempField");
        exprAttrNames.put("#created", "created");
        
        ObjectNode exprAttrValues = mapper.createObjectNode();
        ObjectNode newEntries = mapper.createObjectNode(); newEntries.put("S", "updated entries");
        ObjectNode isActiveTrue = mapper.createObjectNode(); isActiveTrue.put("BOOL", true);
        exprAttrValues.set(":entries", newEntries);
        exprAttrValues.set(":isActive", isActiveTrue);
        
        String updateExpression = "SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created";
        
        System.out.println("\nApplying update expression: " + updateExpression);
        
        DynamoDbService.UpdateResult updateResult = service.updateItem(
            "test-boolean-fix", key, null,
            updateExpression, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues, "ALL_NEW");
        
        System.out.println("Update result attributes: " + updateResult.attributes());
        
        // Step 3: Get the item to verify persistence
        JsonNode finalItem = service.getItem("test-boolean-fix", key);
        System.out.println("\nFinal item: " + finalItem);
        System.out.println("isActive present in final: " + (finalItem != null && finalItem.has("isActive")));
        if (finalItem != null && finalItem.has("isActive")) {
            System.out.println("isActive value: " + finalItem.get("isActive"));
            System.out.println("isActive BOOL: " + finalItem.get("isActive").get("BOOL"));
        }
        System.out.println("entries value: " + (finalItem != null ? finalItem.get("entries") : "null"));
        System.out.println("tempField present: " + (finalItem != null && finalItem.has("tempField")));
        System.out.println("created present: " + (finalItem != null && finalItem.has("created")));
        
        // Check if the bug is present
        if (finalItem == null || !finalItem.has("isActive") || !finalItem.get("isActive").has("BOOL") || finalItem.get("isActive").get("BOOL").asBoolean() != true) {
            System.out.println("\nBUG REPRODUCED: isActive should be true but is not!");
            System.exit(1);
        } else {
            System.out.println("\nTEST PASSED: isActive correctly set to true!");
        }
    }
}
EOF

package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb;

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.InMemoryStorage;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.AttributeDefinition;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.KeySchemaElement;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.util.List;

public class ReproduceTest {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        DynamoDbService service = new DynamoDbService(new InMemoryStorage<>());
        ObjectMapper mapper = new ObjectMapper();
        
        // Create table
        service.createTable("test-boolean-fix",
                List.of(new KeySchemaElement("userId", "HASH")),
                List.of(new AttributeDefinition("userId", "S")),
                5L, 5L);
        
        // Step 1: Create item WITHOUT the boolean field
        ObjectNode putItem = mapper.createObjectNode();
        ObjectNode userIdVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); userIdVal.put("S", "user-123");
        ObjectNode entriesVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); entriesVal.put("S", "initial entries");
        ObjectNode createdVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); createdVal.put("N", "1234567890");
        ObjectNode tempFieldVal = mapper.createObjectNode(); tempFieldVal.put("S", "to be removed");
        putItem.set("userId", userIdVal);
        putItem.set("entries", entriesVal);
        putItem.set("created", createdVal);
        putItem.set("tempField", tempFieldVal);
        service.putItem("test-boolean-fix", putItem);
        
        // Verify initial state
        ObjectNode key = mapper.createObjectNode();
        ObjectNode keyUserId = mapper.createObjectNode(); keyUserId.put("S", "user-123");
        key.set("userId", keyUserId);
        JsonNode initial = service.getItem("test-boolean-fix", key);
        System.out.println("Initial item: " + initial);
        System.out.println("isActive present initially: " + (initial != null && initial.has("isActive")));
        System.out.println("tempField present initially: " + (initial != null && initial.has("tempField")));
        System.out.println("created present initially: " + (initial != null && initial.has("created")));
        
        // Step 2: Update with SET and REMOVE combined (like Enhanced Client does)
        ObjectNode exprAttrNames = mapper.createObjectNode();
        exprAttrNames.put("#entries", "entries");
        exprAttrNames.put("#isActive", "isActive");
        exprAttrNames.put("#tempField", "tempField");
        exprAttrNames.put("#created", "created");
        
        ObjectNode exprAttrValues = mapper.createObjectNode();
        ObjectNode newEntries = mapper.createObjectNode(); newEntries.put("S", "updated entries");
        ObjectNode isActiveTrue = mapper.createObjectNode(); isActiveTrue.put("BOOL", true);
        exprAttrValues.set(":entries", newEntries);
        exprAttrValues.set(":isActive", isActiveTrue);
        
        String updateExpression = "SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created";
        
        System.out.println("\nApplying update expression: " + updateExpression);
        
        DynamoDbService.UpdateResult updateResult = service.updateItem(
            "test-boolean-fix", key, null,
            updateExpression, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues, "ALL_NEW");
        
        System.out.println("Update result newItem: " + updateResult.newItem());
        
        // Step 3: Get the item to verify persistence
        JsonNode finalItem = service.getItem("test-boolean-fix", key);
        System.out.println("\nFinal item: " + finalItem);
        System.out.println("isActive present in final: " + (finalItem != null && finalItem.has("isActive")));
        if (finalItem != null && finalItem.has("isActive")) {
            System.out.println("isActive value: " + finalItem.get("isActive"));
            if (finalItem.get("isActive").has("BOOL")) {
                System.out.println("isActive BOOL: " + finalItem.get("isActive").get("BOOL"));
            }
        }
        System.out.println("entries value: " + (finalItem != null ? finalItem.get("entries") : "null"));
        System.out.println("tempField present: " + (finalItem != null && finalItem.has("tempField")));
        System.out.println("created present: " + (finalItem != null && finalItem.has("created")));
        
        // Check if the bug is present
        if (finalItem == null || !finalItem.has("isActive") || !finalItem.get("isActive").has("BOOL") || finalItem.get("isActive").get("BOOL").asBoolean() != true) {
            System.out.println("\nBUG REPRODUCED: isActive should be true but is not!");
            System.exit(1);
        } else {
            System.out.println("\nTEST PASSED: isActive correctly set to true!");
        }
    }
}
EOF

   877	    private void applyUpdateExpression(ObjectNode item, String expression,
   878	                                        JsonNode exprAttrNames, JsonNode exprAttrValues) {
   879	        // Parse SET and REMOVE clauses from expressions like:
   880	        // "SET #n = :newName, age = :newAge REMOVE oldField"
   881	        String remaining = expression.trim();
   882	
   883	        while (!remaining.isEmpty()) {
   884	            String upper = remaining.toUpperCase();
   885	            if (upper.startsWith("SET ")) {
   886	                remaining = remaining.substring(4).trim();
   887	                remaining = applySetClause(item, remaining, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues);
   888	            } else if (upper.startsWith("REMOVE ")) {
   889	                remaining = remaining.substring(7).trim();
   890	                remaining = applyRemoveClause(item, remaining, exprAttrNames);
   891	            } else if (upper.startsWith("ADD ")) {
   892	                remaining = remaining.substring(4).trim();
   893	                remaining = applyAddClause(item, remaining, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues);
   894	            } else if (upper.startsWith("DELETE ")) {
   895	                // DELETE is for sets — skip for now
   896	                break;
   897	            } else {
   898	                break;
   899	            }
   900	        }
   901	    }
   902	
   903	    private String applySetClause(ObjectNode item, String clause,
   904	                                   JsonNode exprAttrNames, JsonNode exprAttrValues) {
   905	        // Parse comma-separated assignments: "attr = :val, #name = :val2"

2026-05-30 03:19:42,550 - INFO - swea-agent-floci-io__floci-309 - 💭 THOUGHT
Let me trace through the parsing manually:

Input expression: `"SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created"`

1. `applyUpdateExpression` is called with `expression = "SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created"`
   - `remaining = "SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created"`
   - `upper = "SET #ENTRIES = :ENTRIES, #ISACTIVE = :ISACTIVE REMOVE #TEMPField, #CREATED"`
   - Starts with "SET " -> yes
   - `remaining = "#entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created"`
   - Calls `applySetClause(item, "#entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created", ...)`

2. In `applySetClause`:
   - First iteration: `upper = "#entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created".toUpperCase()` = `"#ENTRIES = :ENTRIES, #ISACTIVE = :ISACTIVE REMOVE #TEMPField, #CREATED"`
   - Not starting with REMOVE/ADD/DELETE -> continue
   - `eqIdx = 9` (position of `=` in "#entries = :entries,...")
   - `attrPath = "#entries"`
   - `attrName = resolveAttributeName("#entries", exprAttrNames)` -> `"entries"`
   - `rest = ":entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created"`
   - `commaIdx = findNextComma(":entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created")`
   - In `findNextComma`, scanning: `:entries, ` -> comma at index 8. Returns 8.
   - `valuePart = ":entries"`
   - `rest = "#isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created"`
   - `valuePart` starts with ":" -> resolves `:entries` from exprAttrValues -> sets `entries` to `"updated entries"`
   - `clause = "#isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created"`

   - Second iteration: `upper = "#ISACTIVE = :ISACTIVE REMOVE #TEMPField, #CREATED"`
   - Not starting with REMOVE/ADD/DELETE -> continue
   - `eqIdx = 10` (position of `=` in "#isActive = :isActive REMOVE...")
   - `attrPath = "#isActive"`
   - `attrName = resolveAttributeName("#isActive", exprAttrNames)` -> `"isActive"`
   - `rest = ":isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created"`
   - `commaIdx = findNextComma(":isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created")` 
   - In `findNextComma`, scanning: `:isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created` -> comma at index 23 (before `#created`). Returns 23!
   
   **THAT'S THE BUG!** The `findNextComma` finds the comma before `#created` at index 23, so:
   - `valuePart = ":isActive REMOVE #tempField"` 
   - `rest = "#created"`
   - Now `valuePart` is `":isActive REMOVE #tempField"` which doesn't start with `:` properly, so it goes to the `else if (!valuePart.isEmpty())` branch and tries to resolve it as an attribute reference, failing silently.

So the problem is that `findNextComma` finds a comma that's actually part of the REMOVE clause, not the SET clause. The SET clause parsing should stop when it encounters the REMOVE keyword, but it doesn't check for clause keywords before looking for commas.

Looking at the code flow more carefully:

```java
int commaIdx = findNextComma(rest);
if (commaIdx >= 0) {
    valuePart = rest.substring(0, commaIdx).trim();
    rest = rest.substring(commaIdx + 1).trim();
} else {
    int nextClause = findNextClauseKeyword(rest);
    ...
}
```

So when there IS a comma found, it uses it. But the problem is that `findNextComma` finds a comma that is AFTER a clause keyword boundary. The code should first check if there's a clause keyword before the comma, and if so, treat that as the boundary.

Actually wait, let me re-read the logic. The first check in the while loop is:

```java
if (upper.startsWith("REMOVE ") || upper.startsWith("ADD ") || upper.startsWith("DELETE ")) {
    break;
}
```

But `upper` is `"#ISACTIVE = :ISACTIVE REMOVE #TEMPField, #CREATED"` which starts with `#ISACTIVE`, not `REMOVE`. So it doesn't break. Then `rest` becomes `":isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created"`, and `findNextComma` finds the comma at index 23 (after `#tempField`).

The fix should be: when looking for the comma in the value part, we should also check for clause keywords that might appear before the comma. If a clause keyword appears before the comma, we should stop at that keyword instead.

Let me look at the code again:

```java
// Find the value placeholder or expression
String valuePart;
int commaIdx = findNextComma(rest);
if (commaIdx >= 0) {
    valuePart = rest.substring(0, commaIdx).trim();
    rest = rest.substring(commaIdx + 1).trim();
} else {
    // Check for next clause keyword
    int nextClause = findNextClauseKeyword(rest);
    if (nextClause >= 0) {
        valuePart = rest.substring(0, nextClause).trim();
        rest = rest.substring(nextClause).trim();
    } else {
        valuePart = rest.trim();
        rest = "";
    }
}
```

The fix should be: when `commaIdx >= 0`, also check for `nextClause` and if `nextClause >= 0 && nextClause < commaIdx`, use the clause keyword boundary instead of the comma.

Let me also check the same for `applyRemoveClause`:

```java
int commaIdx = findNextComma(clause);
String attrPart;
if (commaIdx >= 0) {
    attrPart = clause.substring(0, commaIdx).trim();
    clause = clause.substring(commaIdx + 1).trim();
} else {
    int nextClause = findNextClauseKeyword(clause);
    ...
}
```

This has the same issue: if a comma is found after a clause keyword (e.g., `#tempField, #created REMOVE ...`), it would incorrectly split at the comma after `#created` when there's a REMOVE keyword before it.

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/ReproduceEdgeCases.java << 'EOF'
package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb;

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.InMemoryStorage;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.AttributeDefinition;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.KeySchemaElement;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.util.List;

public class ReproduceEdgeCases {
    static ObjectMapper mapper = new ObjectMapper();
    
    static ObjectNode strVal(String v) {
        ObjectNode n = mapper.createObjectNode(); n.put("S", v); return n;
    }
    static ObjectNode boolVal(boolean v) {
        ObjectNode n = mapper.createObjectNode(); n.put("BOOL", v); return n;
    }
    static ObjectNode numVal(String v) {
        ObjectNode n = mapper.createObjectNode(); n.put("N", v); return n;
    }
    
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        int passed = 0, failed = 0;
        
        // Test 1: SET with REMOVE (the original bug)
        if (testSetWithRemove()) { passed++; } else { failed++; System.out.println("FAILED: Test 1"); }
        
        // Test 2: SET only (regression)
        if (testSetOnly()) { passed++; } else { failed++; System.out.println("FAILED: Test 2"); }
        
        // Test 3: REMOVE only (regression)
        if (testRemoveOnly()) { passed++; } else { failed++; System.out.println("FAILED: Test 3"); }
        
        // Test 4: SET with multiple REMOVE attributes
        if (testSetWithMultiRemove()) { passed++; } else { failed++; System.out.println("FAILED: Test 4"); }
        
        // Test 5: Multiple SET with REMOVE
        if (testMultiSetWithRemove()) { passed++; } else { failed++; System.out.println("FAILED: Test 5"); }
        
        // Test 6: Boolean false to true (from PR description second scenario)
        if (testBoolFalseToTrue()) { passed++; } else { failed++; System.out.println("FAILED: Test 6"); }
        
        // Test 7: SET with if_not_exists and REMOVE
        if (testSetIfNotExistsWithRemove()) { passed++; } else { failed++; System.out.println("FAILED: Test 7"); }
        
        System.out.println("\n" + passed + "/" + (passed + failed) + " tests passed.");
        if (failed > 0) System.exit(1);
    }
    
    static DynamoDbService createService(String tableName) {
        DynamoDbService svc = new DynamoDbService(new InMemoryStorage<>());
        svc.createTable(tableName,
                List.of(new KeySchemaElement("userId", "HASH")),
                List.of(new AttributeDefinition("userId", "S")),
                5L, 5L);
        return svc;
    }
    
    static ObjectNode key(String userId) {
        ObjectNode k = mapper.createObjectNode();
        k.set("userId", strVal(userId));
        return k;
    }
    
    // Test 1: SET with REMOVE (original bug)
    static boolean testSetWithRemove() {
        DynamoDbService svc = createService("test1");
        
        // Put initial item with fields
        ObjectNode item = mapper.createObjectNode();
        item.set("userId", strVal("u1"));
        item.set("entries", strVal("initial"));
        item.set("tempField", strVal("temp"));
        item.set("created", numVal("123"));
        svc.putItem("test1", item);
        
        // Update: SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created
        ObjectNode names = mapper.createObjectNode();
        names.put("#entries", "entries");
        names.put("#isActive", "isActive");
        names.put("#tempField", "tempField");
        names.put("#created", "created");
        
        ObjectNode values = mapper.createObjectNode();
        values.set(":entries", strVal("updated"));
        values.set(":isActive", boolVal(true));
        
        svc.updateItem("test1", key("u1"), null,
            "SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField, #created",
            names, values, "ALL_NEW");
        
        JsonNode result = svc.getItem("test1", key("u1"));
        return result.has("isActive") && result.get("isActive").get("BOOL").asBoolean() == true
            && result.get("entries").get("S").asText().equals("updated")
            && !result.has("tempField")
            && !result.has("created");
    }
    
    // Test 2: SET only
    static boolean testSetOnly() {
        DynamoDbService svc = createService("test2");
        ObjectNode item = mapper.createObjectNode();
        item.set("userId", strVal("u2"));
        item.set("name", strVal("old"));
        svc.putItem("test2", item);
        
        ObjectNode values = mapper.createObjectNode();
        values.set(":name", strVal("new"));
        
        svc.updateItem("test2", key("u2"), null,
            "SET name = :name", null, values, "ALL_NEW");
        
        JsonNode result = svc.getItem("test2", key("u2"));
        return result.get("name").get("S").asText().equals("new");
    }
    
    // Test 3: REMOVE only
    static boolean testRemoveOnly() {
        DynamoDbService svc = createService("test3");
        ObjectNode item = mapper.createObjectNode();
        item.set("userId", strVal("u3"));
        item.set("field1", strVal("val1"));
        item.set("field2", strVal("val2"));
        svc.putItem("test3", item);
        
        ObjectNode names = mapper.createObjectNode();
        names.put("#f1", "field1");
        names.put("#f2", "field2");
        
        svc.updateItem("test3", key("u3"), null,
            "REMOVE #f1, #f2", names, null, "ALL_NEW");
        
        JsonNode result = svc.getItem("test3", key("u3"));
        return !result.has("field1") && !result.has("field2");
    }
    
    // Test 4: SET with multiple REMOVE attributes
    static boolean testSetWithMultiRemove() {
        DynamoDbService svc = createService("test4");
        ObjectNode item = mapper.createObjectNode();
        item.set("userId", strVal("u4"));
        item.set("a", strVal("oldA"));
        item.set("b", strVal("oldB"));
        item.set("c", strVal("oldC"));
        svc.putItem("test4", item);
        
        ObjectNode values = mapper.createObjectNode();
        values.set(":a", strVal("newA"));
        
        svc.updateItem("test4", key("u4"), null,
            "SET a = :a REMOVE b, c", null, values, "ALL_NEW");
        
        JsonNode result = svc.getItem("test4", key("u4"));
        return result.get("a").get("S").asText().equals("newA")
            && !result.has("b")
            && !result.has("c");
    }
    
    // Test 5: Multiple SET with REMOVE
    static boolean testMultiSetWithRemove() {
        DynamoDbService svc = createService("test5");
        ObjectNode item = mapper.createObjectNode();
        item.set("userId", strVal("u5"));
        item.set("a", strVal("oldA"));
        item.set("b", strVal("oldB"));
        item.set("c", strVal("oldC"));
        svc.putItem("test5", item);
        
        ObjectNode names = mapper.createObjectNode();
        names.put("#a", "a");
        names.put("#b", "b");
        names.put("#c", "c");
        
        ObjectNode values = mapper.createObjectNode();
        values.set(":a", strVal("newA"));
        values.set(":b", strVal("newB"));
        
        svc.updateItem("test5", key("u5"), null,
            "SET #a = :a, #b = :b REMOVE #c", names, values, "ALL_NEW");
        
        JsonNode result = svc.getItem("test5", key("u5"));
        return result.get("a").get("S").asText().equals("newA")
            && result.get("b").get("S").asText().equals("newB")
            && !result.has("c");
    }
    
    // Test 6: Boolean false to true
    static boolean testBoolFalseToTrue() {
        DynamoDbService svc = createService("test6");
        ObjectNode item = mapper.createObjectNode();
        item.set("userId", strVal("u6"));
        item.set("entries", strVal("initial"));
        item.set("isActive", boolVal(false));
        item.set("tempField", strVal("temp"));
        svc.putItem("test6", item);
        
        ObjectNode names = mapper.createObjectNode();
        names.put("#entries", "entries");
        names.put("#isActive", "isActive");
        names.put("#tempField", "tempField");
        
        ObjectNode values = mapper.createObjectNode();
        values.set(":entries", strVal("updated"));
        values.set(":isActive", boolVal(true));
        
        svc.updateItem("test6", key("u6"), null,
            "SET #entries = :entries, #isActive = :isActive REMOVE #tempField",
            names, values, "ALL_NEW");
        
        JsonNode result = svc.getItem("test6", key("u6"));
        return result.has("isActive") && result.get("isActive").get("BOOL").asBoolean() == true
            && result.get("entries").get("S").asText().equals("updated")
            && !result.has("tempField");
    }
    
    // Test 7: SET with if_not_exists and REMOVE
    static boolean testSetIfNotExistsWithRemove() {
        DynamoDbService svc = createService("test7");
        ObjectNode item = mapper.createObjectNode();
        item.set("userId", strVal("u7"));
        item.set("toRemove", strVal("bye"));
        svc.putItem("test7", item);
        
        ObjectNode values = mapper.createObjectNode();
        values.set(":val", strVal("default"));
        
        ObjectNode names = mapper.createObjectNode();
        names.put("#tr", "toRemove");
        
        svc.updateItem("test7", key("u7"), null,
            "SET name = if_not_exists(name, :val) REMOVE #tr",
            names, values, "ALL_NEW");
        
        JsonNode result = svc.getItem("test7", key("u7"));
        return result.has("name") && result.get("name").get("S").asText().equals("default")
            && !result.has("toRemove");
    }
}
EOF

package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb;

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.InMemoryStorage;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.AttributeDefinition;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.KeySchemaElement;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.util.List;

public class ReproduceAddEdge {
    static ObjectMapper mapper = new ObjectMapper();
    
    static ObjectNode strVal(String v) {
        ObjectNode n = mapper.createObjectNode(); n.put("S", v); return n;
    }
    static ObjectNode numVal(String v) {
        ObjectNode n = mapper.createObjectNode(); n.put("N", v); return n;
    }
    
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        int passed = 0, failed = 0;
        
        // Test ADD with REMOVE
        if (testAddWithRemove()) { passed++; } else { failed++; System.out.println("FAILED: Test Add+Remove"); }
        
        // Test ADD with SET
        if (testAddWithSet()) { passed++; } else { failed++; System.out.println("FAILED: Test Add+Set"); }
        
        System.out.println("\n" + passed + "/" + (passed + failed) + " tests passed.");
        if (failed > 0) System.exit(1);
    }
    
    static DynamoDbService createService(String tableName) {
        DynamoDbService svc = new DynamoDbService(new InMemoryStorage<>());
        svc.createTable(tableName,
                List.of(new KeySchemaElement("userId", "HASH")),
                List.of(new AttributeDefinition("userId", "S")),
                5L, 5L);
        return svc;
    }
    
    static ObjectNode key(String userId) {
        ObjectNode k = mapper.createObjectNode();
        k.set("userId", strVal(userId));
        return k;
    }
    
    static boolean testAddWithRemove() {
        DynamoDbService svc = createService("addRemove");
        ObjectNode item = mapper.createObjectNode();
        item.set("userId", strVal("u1"));
        item.set("counter", numVal("10"));
        item.set("temp", strVal("bye"));
        svc.putItem("addRemove", item);
        
        ObjectNode values = mapper.createObjectNode();
        values.set(":inc", numVal("5"));
        
        svc.updateItem("addRemove", key("u1"), null,
            "ADD counter :inc REMOVE temp", null, values, "ALL_NEW");
        
        JsonNode result = svc.getItem("addRemove", key("u1"));
        return result.get("counter").get("N").asText().equals("15")
            && !result.has("temp");
    }
    
    static boolean testAddWithSet() {
        DynamoDbService svc = createService("addSet");
        ObjectNode item = mapper.createObjectNode();
        item.set("userId", strVal("u2"));
        item.set("counter", numVal("10"));
        item.set("name", strVal("old"));
        svc.putItem("addSet", item);
        
        ObjectNode values = mapper.createObjectNode();
        values.set(":inc", numVal("5"));
        values.set(":name", strVal("new"));
        
        svc.updateItem("addSet", key("u2"), null,
            "SET name = :name ADD counter :inc", null, values, "ALL_NEW");
        
        JsonNode result = svc.getItem("addSet", key("u2"));
        return result.get("counter").get("N").asText().equals("15")
            && result.get("name").get("S").asText().equals("new");
    }
}

   903	    private String applySetClause(ObjectNode item, String clause,
   904	                                   JsonNode exprAttrNames, JsonNode exprAttrValues) {
   905	        // Parse comma-separated assignments: "attr = :val, #name = :val2"
   906	        // Stop when we hit another clause keyword (REMOVE, ADD, DELETE) or end
   907	        while (!clause.isEmpty()) {
   908	            String upper = clause.toUpperCase();
   909	            if (upper.startsWith("REMOVE ") || upper.startsWith("ADD ") || upper.startsWith("DELETE ")) {
   910	                break;
   911	            }
   912	
   913	            // Parse "attrPath = valueExpr"
   914	            int eqIdx = clause.indexOf('=');
   915	            if (eqIdx < 0) break;
   916	
   917	            String attrPath = clause.substring(0, eqIdx).trim();
   918	            String attrName = resolveAttributeName(attrPath, exprAttrNames);
   919	
   920	            String rest = clause.substring(eqIdx + 1).trim();
   921	
   922	            // Find the value placeholder or expression
   923	            String valuePart;
   924	            int commaIdx = findNextComma(rest);
   925	            int nextClause = findNextClauseKeyword(rest);
   926	            
   927	            // Use the nearest boundary (comma or next clause keyword)
   928	            if (commaIdx >= 0 && (nextClause < 0 || commaIdx < nextClause)) {
   929	                valuePart = rest.substring(0, commaIdx).trim();
   930	                rest = rest.substring(commaIdx + 1).trim();
   931	            } else if (nextClause >= 0) {
   932	                valuePart = rest.substring(0, nextClause).trim();
   933	                rest = rest.substring(nextClause).trim();
   934	            } else {
   935	                valuePart = rest.trim();
   936	                rest = "";
   937	            }
   938	
   939	            // Resolve the value
   940	            if (valuePart.startsWith("if_not_exists(")) {
   941	                // if_not_exists(attrRef, fallbackExpr) evaluates to:
   942	                //   attrRef's current value  — when attrRef exists in the item
   943	                //   fallbackExpr             — otherwise
   944	                // The result is always assigned to attrName.
   945	                String[] args = extractFunctionArgs(valuePart);
   946	                if (args.length == 2) {
   947	                    String checkAttr = resolveAttributeName(args[0].trim(), exprAttrNames);
   948	                    String fallbackExpr = args[1].trim();
   949	                    JsonNode resolved;
   950	                    if (item.has(checkAttr)) {
   951	                        // attrRef exists — evaluate to its current value
   952	                        resolved = item.get(checkAttr);
   953	                    } else if (fallbackExpr.startsWith(":") && exprAttrValues != null) {
   954	                        resolved = exprAttrValues.get(fallbackExpr);
   955	                    } else {
   956	                        // fallback is itself an attribute reference
   957	                        resolved = item.get(resolveAttributeName(fallbackExpr, exprAttrNames));
   958	                    }
   959	                    if (resolved != null) {
   960	                        item.set(attrName, resolved);
   961	                    }
   962	                }
   963	            } else if (valuePart.startsWith("list_append(")) {
   964	                String[] args = extractFunctionArgs(valuePart);
   965	                if (args.length == 2) {
   966	                    String arg1 = args[0].trim();
   967	                    String arg2 = args[1].trim();
   968	                    JsonNode list1 = arg1.startsWith(":") && exprAttrValues != null
   969	                        ? exprAttrValues.get(arg1)
   970	                        : item.get(resolveAttributeName(arg1, exprAttrNames));
   971	                    JsonNode list2 = arg2.startsWith(":") && exprAttrValues != null
   972	                        ? exprAttrValues.get(arg2)
   973	                        : item.get(resolveAttributeName(arg2, exprAttrNames));
   974	                    if (list1 != null && list2 != null && list1.has("L") && list2.has("L")) {
   975	                        com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ArrayNode merged =
   976	                            com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.JsonNodeFactory.instance.arrayNode();
   977	                        list1.get("L").forEach(merged::add);
   978	                        list2.get("L").forEach(merged::add);
   979	                        com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode result =
   980	                            com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.JsonNodeFactory.instance.objectNode();
   981	                        result.set("L", merged);
   982	                        item.set(attrName, result);
   983	                    }
   984	                }
   985	            } else if (valuePart.startsWith(":") && exprAttrValues != null) {
   986	                JsonNode value = exprAttrValues.get(valuePart);
   987	                if (value != null) {
   988	                    item.set(attrName, value);
   989	                }
   990	            } else if (!valuePart.isEmpty()) {
   991	                // Plain attribute reference: SET a = b  or  SET a = #alias
   992	                String refAttr = resolveAttributeName(valuePart, exprAttrNames);
   993	                JsonNode refValue = item.get(refAttr);
   994	                if (refValue != null) {
   995	                    item.set(attrName, refValue);
   996	                }
   997	            }
   998	
   999	            clause = rest;
  1000	        }
  1001	        return clause;
  1002	    }
